  <script type="text/javascript">
   function show_dialog(show_id){
            if ($('#'+ show_id).length>0){

                if ($('.boxDialog:visible').length>0){
                    $('.boxDialog:visible').each(function(){
                      $(this).animate({'top':-1*$(this).height()+ 'px', 'display':'none'},500,function(){
                          $(this).hide();
                          //$('.overlay').fadeOut('fast');
                      });
                    });
                }

                $('.overlay').fadeIn('fast',function(){
                    var height = ($(window).height()-$('#'+ show_id).height())/2;
                    if(height<0) height = 0;
                    $('#'+ show_id).show().animate({'top':height+'px'},500);
                });

            }
        }


        $(function() {

            $('.hasDialog').click(function(){
                var show_id = $(this).attr('dialog');
                show_dialog(show_id);
            });

            $('.boxclose, .boxclose_unstyled').click(function(){
                var box_dialog = $(this).parents('.boxDialog').eq(0);
                $(box_dialog).animate({'top':-1*$(box_dialog).height()+ 'px', 'display':'none'},500,function(){
                    $(this).hide();
                    $('.overlay').fadeOut('fast');
                });
                $(box_dialog).remove();
            });

            $('.boxDialog').each(function(){
                $(this).css({ 'top': -1*$(this).height()+'px'}).hide();
            });


            show_dialog('box10');

        });
  </script>
  <style>
   .box10{

        }

      async function toggleMenu() {
                var x = document.getElementById('catalogo');
                if (x.style.display === 'none') {
                    x.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    x.style.display = 'none';
                }
            }

        <script language="javascript">
         async function redirect_menu() {
                                var current_url = window.top.location.href.substring(window.top.location.href.indexOf('/', 7));
                                var selected_url = document.getElementById("catalogo_select").value;
                                if (current_url != selected_url) window.top.location.href = selected_url;
                            }
                            var touchzone = document.getElementById("catalogo_select");

                            touchzone.addEventListener("change", redirect_menu, false);
        </script>

    $(function() {
        $("#products").autocomplete({
            source: "/api/get_products/",
            minLength: 1,
            delay: 500,
            select:function(event, ui) { 
                location.href = ui.item.url;
            },
            open: function(event, ui) {
                $(".ui-autocomplete").css("z-index", 1000);
            },
            create: function () {
                $(this).data( "autocomplete" )._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {
                    return $( "<li></li>" )
                    .data( "item.autocomplete", item )
                    .attr( "id", item.value )
                    .append( "<a href=\""+item.url+"\">" + item.value + "</a>" )
                    .appendTo( ul );
                }
            }
        });

        $("#products").autocomplete("widget").addClass('yourclass');

    });
   </script>

    function escondersubmenu(id){
        $( '.family_nav').each(function( index ) {
            $(this).hide();
        });
    }

    function mostrasubmenu(id){
        console.log('teste');
        for (var i=0; i<allsubmenus.length; i++) {
            if (allsubmenus[i] != id) {
                $('#submenu'+allsubmenus[i]).hide();
            }
        }
        for (var i=0; i<allsubsubmenus.length; i++) {
            if ($('#submenu'+id+' #subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]+'.togg').length) {
                $('#submenu'+id+' #subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]+'.togg').children('#type2').slideToggle();
                $('#submenu'+id+' #subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]).toggleClass('togg');
            }
        }
        $('#submenu'+id).toggle(null, function(){

            $('#submenu'+id).bind( "clickoutside", function(event){
                for (var i=0; i<allsubsubmenus.length; i++) {
                    if ($('#submenu'+id+' #subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]+'.togg').length) {
                        $('#submenu'+id+' #subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]+'.togg').children('#type2').slideToggle();
                        $('#submenu'+id+' #subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]).toggleClass('togg');
                    }
                }
                $('#submenu'+id).toggle();
                $('#submenu'+id).unbind( "clickoutside");
            });
        });


    }

    function mostrasubsubmenu(id) {
        for (var i=0; i<allsubsubmenus.length; i++) {
            if (allsubsubmenus[i] != id) {
                if ($('#subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]+'.togg').length) {
                    $('#subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]+'.togg').children('#type2').slideToggle();
                    $('#subsubmenu'+allsubsubmenus[i]).toggleClass('togg');
                }
            }
        }
        $('#subsubmenu'+id).toggleClass('togg');
        $('#subsubmenu'+id).children('#type2').slideToggle();
    }
   </script>

      <script>
       function ee(f){errors='';$.each(f, function (key, element) {errors+=element+'<br>';});return errors;}

                $(document).ready(function(){
                    /* attach a submit handler to the form */
                    $("#newsletter_register").submit(function(event) {
                        $('.newsletter_register_msgs div span').html('');
                        $('.newsletter_register_msgs div').hide();

                        event.preventDefault();
                        $.post( '/newsletter/subscribe/',  $("#newsletter_register").serialize() ,'json').done(function(data) {
                            $('#newsletter_register').find('input[type=text]').val('');
                            $('.newsletter_register_msgs div span.form_sucess').html('O seu pedido foi registado com sucesso.<br> Por favor verifique o seu email.').parent().show();
                        }).fail(function(data) {
                            if (jQuery.parseJSON(data.responseText).errors.__all__!=undefined){
                                $('.newsletter_register_msgs').find('span.__all__').html(ee(jQuery.parseJSON(data.responseText).errors.__all__)).show();
                                delete jQuery.parseJSON(data.responseText).errors.__all__;
                            }
                            $.each(jQuery.parseJSON(data.responseText).errors, function (key, element) {
                                $('.newsletter_register_msgs').find('span.'+key+'_form_erros').html(ee(element)).parent().show();
                            });
                        });
                    });
                });
      </script>

            function new_quantity(elem){
                tamanho = $(elem).val();

                $(elem).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('select[name^=quantity]').parent('div').hide();
                /*
                $(elem).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('select[name=quantity'+tamanho+']').parent('div').show();
                $(elem).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('input[name=quantity]').val($('select[name=quantity'+tamanho+']').val());
                */
                $(elem).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('input[name=quantity'+tamanho+']').parent('div').show();
                $(elem).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('input[name=quantity]').val($('input[name=quantity'+tamanho+']').val());
            }

            $(document).ready(function() {

                $.each($('.parentsizeselect'), function(index, value) {

                    var b_form = $(this).find(".basket_form");
                    var select_size = $(this).find('.select_size');
                    var select_size2 = $(this).find('select[name=product_id]');
                    b_form.find('div.bt_basket').click(function(){
                        if(select_size.val() != undefined && select_size.val()!="" ){
                            b_form.submit();
                        }else{
                            show_dialog('box3');
                        }
                    });

                    select_size.bind('change', function() {
                        select_size2.val($(this).val());
                    });

                    
                    $(this).find('select[name=product_id]').val(select_size.val());
                    $(this).find('input[name=quantity]').val($(this).find('input[name=quantity'+$(this).find('.select_size').val()+']').val());
                    $(this).find('input[name^=quantity]').parent('div').hide();
                    $(this).find('input[name=quantity'+$(this).find('.select_size').val()+']').parent('div').show();
                    $(this).find('.qty_info').show();
                    $.each($(this).find('input[name^=quantity]').not("input[name=quantity]"), function(index2, value2) {
                        $(this).bind('change', function() {
                            $(this).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('input[name=quantity]').val($(this).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('input[name=quantity'+$(this).parents('.parentsizeselect').find('.select_size').val()+']').val());
                        });
                    });

                });


                $(".price_add").click(function() {

                    showdialog = $(this).parents('.parentproduct').find('.boxaddcarrinho');

                    if (showdialog.length>0){

                        if ($('.boxDialog:visible').length>0){
                            $('.boxDialog:visible').each(function(){
                              $(this).animate({'top':-1*$(this).height()+ 'px', 'display':'none'},500,function(){
                                  $(this).hide();
                                  //$('.overlay').fadeOut('fast');
                              });
                            });
                        }

                        $('.overlay').fadeIn('fast',function(){
                            var height = ($(window).height()-showdialog.height())/2;
                            if(height<0) height = 0;
                            showdialog.show().animate({'top':height+'px'},500);
                        });

                    }

                });

            });

            $( window ).resize(function() {
                if ($('.boxDialog:visible').length>0){

                    var height = ($(window).height()-$('.boxDialog:visible').find('.pop_txtaddcarrinho').prop('scrollHeight'))/2;

                    if(height-30<0){
                        height = 30;
                        $('.boxDialog:visible').attr("style", "display: block; overflow: hidden; padding-top:30px; height: "+($(window).height()-100) +"px; top:"+height+"px");
                        $('.boxDialog:visible').find('.pop_txtaddcarrinho').attr("style", "overflow-y: scroll; overflow-x: hidden; height: "+($(window).height()-105) +"px;");
                    }else{
                        $('.boxDialog:visible').attr("style", "display: block; overflow: hidden; padding-top:30px; height: "+$('.boxDialog:visible').find('.pop_txtaddcarrinho').prop('scrollHeight') +"px; top:"+height+"px");
                        $('.boxDialog:visible').find('.pop_txtaddcarrinho').attr("style", "overflow-x: hidden; overflow-y: auto; top:"+height+"px;");
                    }
                    //$('.boxDialog:visible').show().animate({'top':height+'px'},500);
                }
            });
  </script>
